37/* FCGI Connection flags (32 bits) */
38#define FCGI_CF_NONE0x00000000 0x00000000
39
40/* Flags indicating why writing to the mux is blockes */
41#define FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001 0x00000001 /* mux is blocked on lack connection's mux buffer */
42#define FCGI_CF_MUX_MFULL0x00000002 0x00000002 /* mux is blocked on connection's mux buffer full */
43#define FCGI_CF_MUX_BLOCK_ANY0x00000003 0x00000003 /* mux is blocked on connection's mux buffer full */
44
45/* Flags indicating why writing to the demux is blocked.
46 * The first two ones directly affect the ability for the mux to receive data
47 * from the connection. The other ones affect the mux's ability to demux
48 * received data.
49 */
50#define FCGI_CF_DEM_DALLOC0x00000004 0x00000004 /* demux blocked on lack of connection's demux buffer */
51#define FCGI_CF_DEM_DFULL0x00000008 0x00000008 /* demux blocked on connection's demux buffer full */
52#define FCGI_CF_DEM_MROOM0x00000010 0x00000010 /* demux blocked on lack of room in mux buffer */
53#define FCGI_CF_DEM_SALLOC0x00000020 0x00000020 /* demux blocked on lack of stream's rx buffer */
54#define FCGI_CF_DEM_SFULL0x00000040 0x00000040 /* demux blocked on stream request buffer full */
55#define FCGI_CF_DEM_TOOMANY0x00000080 0x00000080 /* demux blocked waiting for some conn_streams to leave */
56#define FCGI_CF_DEM_BLOCK_ANY0x000000F0 0x000000F0 /* aggregate of the demux flags above except DALLOC/DFULL */
57
58/* Other flags */
59#define FCGI_CF_MPXS_CONNS0x00000100 0x00000100 /* connection multiplexing is supported */
60#define FCGI_CF_ABRTS_SENT0x00000200 0x00000200 /* a record ABORT was successfully sent to all active streams */
61#define FCGI_CF_ABRTS_FAILED0x00000400 0x00000400 /* failed to abort processing of all streams */
62#define FCGI_CF_WAIT_FOR_HS0x00000800 0x00000800 /* We did check that at least a stream was waiting for handshake */
63#define FCGI_CF_KEEP_CONN0x00001000 0x00001000 /* HAproxy is responsible to close the connection */
64#define FCGI_CF_GET_VALUES0x00002000 0x00002000 /* retrieve settings */
65
66/* FCGI connection state (fcgi_conn->state) */
67enum fcgi_conn_st {
68 FCGI_CS_INIT = 0, /* init done, waiting for sending GET_VALUES record */
69 FCGI_CS_SETTINGS, /* GET_VALUES sent, waiting for the GET_VALUES_RESULT record */
70 FCGI_CS_RECORD_H, /* GET_VALUES_RESULT received, waiting for a record header */
71 FCGI_CS_RECORD_D, /* Record header OK, waiting for a record data */
72 FCGI_CS_RECORD_P, /* Record processed, remains the padding */
73 FCGI_CS_CLOSED, /* abort requests if necessary and close the connection ASAP */
74 FCGI_CS_ENTRIES
75} __attribute__((packed));
76
77/* 32 buffers: one for the ring's root, rest for the mbuf itself */
78#define FCGI_C_MBUF_CNT32 32
79
80/* FCGI connection descriptor */
81struct fcgi_conn {
82 struct connection *conn;
83
84 enum fcgi_conn_st state; /* FCGI connection state */
85 int16_t max_id; /* highest ID known on this connection, <0 before mgmt records */
86 uint32_t streams_limit; /* maximum number of concurrent streams the peer supports */
87 uint32_t flags; /* Connection flags: FCGI_CF_* */
88
89 int16_t dsi; /* dmux stream ID (<0 = idle ) */
90 uint16_t drl; /* demux record length (if dsi >= 0) */
91 uint8_t drt; /* demux record type (if dsi >= 0) */
92 uint8_t drp; /* demux record padding (if dsi >= 0) */
93
94 struct buffer dbuf; /* demux buffer */
95 struct buffer mbuf[FCGI_C_MBUF_CNT32]; /* mux buffers (ring) */
96
97 int timeout; /* idle timeout duration in ticks */
98 int shut_timeout; /* idle timeout duration in ticks after shutdown */
99 unsigned int nb_streams; /* number of streams in the tree */
100 unsigned int nb_cs; /* number of attached conn_streams */
101 unsigned int nb_reserved; /* number of reserved streams */
102 unsigned int stream_cnt; /* total number of streams seen */
103
104 struct proxy *proxy; /* the proxy this connection was created for */
105 struct fcgi_app *app; /* FCGI application used by this mux */
106 struct task *task; /* timeout management task */
107 struct eb_root streams_by_id; /* all active streams by their ID */
108
109 struct list send_list; /* list of blocked streams requesting to send */
110
111 struct buffer_wait buf_wait; /* Wait list for buffer allocation */
112 struct wait_event wait_event; /* To be used if we're waiting for I/Os */
113};
114
115
116/* FCGI stream state, in fcgi_strm->state */
117enum fcgi_strm_st {
118 FCGI_SS_IDLE = 0,
119 FCGI_SS_OPEN,
120 FCGI_SS_HREM, // half-closed(remote)
121 FCGI_SS_HLOC, // half-closed(local)
122 FCGI_SS_ERROR,
123 FCGI_SS_CLOSED,
124 FCGI_SS_ENTRIES
125} __attribute__((packed));
126
127
128/* FCGI stream flags (32 bits) */
129#define FCGI_SF_NONE0x00000000 0x00000000
130#define FCGI_SF_ES_RCVD0x00000001 0x00000001 /* end-of-stream received (empty STDOUT or EDN_REQUEST record) */
131#define FCGI_SF_ES_SENT0x00000002 0x00000002 /* end-of-strem sent (empty STDIN record) */
132#define FCGI_SF_ABRT_SENT0x00000004 0x00000004 /* abort sent (ABORT_REQUEST record) */
133
134/* Stream flags indicating the reason the stream is blocked */
135#define FCGI_SF_BLK_MBUSY0x00000010 0x00000010 /* blocked waiting for mux access (transient) */
136#define FCGI_SF_BLK_MROOM0x00000020 0x00000020 /* blocked waiting for room in the mux */
137#define FCGI_SF_BLK_ANY0x00000030 0x00000030 /* any of the reasons above */
138
139#define FCGI_SF_BEGIN_SENT0x00000100 0x00000100 /* a BEGIN_REQUEST record was sent for this stream */
140#define FCGI_SF_OUTGOING_DATA0x00000200 0x00000200 /* set whenever we've seen outgoing data */
141#define FCGI_SF_NOTIFIED0x00000400 0x00000400 /* a paused stream was notified to try to send again */
142
143#define FCGI_SF_WANT_SHUTR0x00001000 0x00001000 /* a stream couldn't shutr() (mux full/busy) */
144#define FCGI_SF_WANT_SHUTW0x00002000 0x00002000 /* a stream couldn't shutw() (mux full/busy) */
145#define FCGI_SF_KILL_CONN0x00004000 0x00004000 /* kill the whole connection with this stream */
146
147/* Other flags */
148#define FCGI_SF_H1_PARSING_DONE0x00010000 0x00010000
149
150/* FCGI stream descriptor */
151struct fcgi_strm {
152 struct conn_stream *cs;
153 struct session *sess;
154 struct fcgi_conn *fconn;
155
156 int32_t id; /* stream ID */
157
158 uint32_t flags; /* Connection flags: FCGI_SF_* */
159 enum fcgi_strm_st state; /* FCGI stream state */
160 int proto_status; /* FCGI_PS_* */
161
162 struct h1m h1m; /* response parser state for H1 */
163
164 struct buffer rxbuf; /* receive buffer, always valid (buf_empty or real buffer) */
165
166 struct eb32_node by_id; /* place in fcgi_conn's streams_by_id */
167 struct wait_event *subs; /* Address of the wait_event the conn_stream associated is waiting on */
168 struct list send_list; /* To be used when adding in fcgi_conn->send_list */
169 struct tasklet *shut_tl; /* deferred shutdown tasklet, to retry to close after we failed to by lack of space */
170};

220/* The event representation is split like this :
221 * fconn - internal FCGI connection
222 * fstrm - internal FCGI stream
223 * strm - application layer
224 * rx - data receipt
225 * tx - data transmission
226 * rsp - response parsing
227 */
228static const struct trace_event fcgi_trace_events[] = {
229#define FCGI_EV_FCONN_NEW(1ULL << 0) (1ULL << 0)
230 { .mask = FCGI_EV_FCONN_NEW(1ULL << 0), .name = "fconn_new", .desc = "new FCGI connection" },
231#define FCGI_EV_FCONN_RECV(1ULL << 1) (1ULL << 1)
232 { .mask = FCGI_EV_FCONN_RECV(1ULL << 1), .name = "fconn_recv", .desc = "Rx on FCGI connection" },
233#define FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND(1ULL << 2) (1ULL << 2)
234 { .mask = FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND(1ULL << 2), .name = "fconn_send", .desc = "Tx on FCGI connection" },
235#define FCGI_EV_FCONN_BLK(1ULL << 3) (1ULL << 3)
236 { .mask = FCGI_EV_FCONN_BLK(1ULL << 3), .name = "fconn_blk", .desc = "FCGI connection blocked" },
237#define FCGI_EV_FCONN_WAKE(1ULL << 4) (1ULL << 4)

336static struct trace_source trace_fcgi = {
337 .name = IST("fcgi"){ .ptr = "fcgi" "", .len = (sizeof "fcgi" "") - 1 },
338 .desc = "FastCGI multiplexer",
339 .arg_def = TRC_ARG1_CONN((1 << 0) << 0), // TRACE()'s first argument is always a connection
340 .default_cb = fcgi_trace,
341 .known_events = fcgi_trace_events,
342 .lockon_args = fcgi_trace_lockon_args,
343 .decoding = fcgi_trace_decoding,
344 .report_events = ~0, // report everything by default
345};

350/* FCGI connection and stream pools */

"__start_init_STG_POOL"); __asm__(".globl " "__stop_init_STG_POOL"

*,void *))create_pool_callback, .arg1 = (void *)((&pool_head_fcgi_conn
)), .arg2 = (void *)(("fcgi_conn")), .arg3 = (void *)((sizeof
(struct fcgi_conn))), } : ((void*)0);
352DECLARE_STATIC_POOL(pool_head_fcgi_strm, "fcgi_strm", sizeof(struct fcgi_strm))static struct pool_head *(pool_head_fcgi_strm); __asm__(".globl "
"__start_init_STG_POOL"); __asm__(".globl " "__stop_init_STG_POOL"
); static const struct initcall *__initcb_352 __attribute__((
__used__,__section__("init_" "STG_POOL"))) = (STG_POOL < STG_SIZE
) ? &(const struct initcall) { .fct = (void (*)(void *,void
*,void *))create_pool_callback, .arg1 = (void *)((&pool_head_fcgi_strm
)), .arg2 = (void *)(("fcgi_strm")), .arg3 = (void *)((sizeof

355static int fcgi_process(struct fcgi_conn *fconn);

365/* a dmumy management stream */
366static const struct fcgi_strm *fcgi_mgmt_stream = &(const struct fcgi_strm){
367 .cs = NULL((void*)0),
368 .fconn = NULL((void*)0),
369 .state = FCGI_SS_CLOSED,
370 .flags = FCGI_SF_NONE0x00000000,
371 .id = 0,
372};
373
374/* and a dummy idle stream for use with any unknown stream */
375static const struct fcgi_strm *fcgi_unknown_stream = &(const struct fcgi_strm){
376 .cs = NULL((void*)0),
377 .fconn = NULL((void*)0),
378 .state = FCGI_SS_IDLE,
379 .flags = FCGI_SF_NONE0x00000000,
380 .id = 0,
381};
382
383/* returns a fconn state as an abbreviated 3-letter string, or "???" if unknown */
384static inline const char *fconn_st_to_str(enum fcgi_conn_st st)
385{
386 switch (st) {
387 case FCGI_CS_INIT : return "INI";
388 case FCGI_CS_SETTINGS : return "STG";
389 case FCGI_CS_RECORD_H : return "RDH";
390 case FCGI_CS_RECORD_D : return "RDD";
391 case FCGI_CS_RECORD_P : return "RDP";
392 case FCGI_CS_CLOSED : return "CLO";
393 default : return "???";
394 }
395}
396
397/* returns a fstrm state as an abbreviated 3-letter string, or "???" if unknown */
398static inline const char *fstrm_st_to_str(enum fcgi_strm_st st)
399{
400 switch (st) {
401 case FCGI_SS_IDLE : return "IDL";
402 case FCGI_SS_OPEN : return "OPN";
403 case FCGI_SS_HREM : return "RCL";
404 case FCGI_SS_HLOC : return "HCL";
405 case FCGI_SS_ERROR : return "ERR";
406 case FCGI_SS_CLOSED : return "CLO";
407 default : return "???";
408 }
409}
410
411
412/* the FCGI traces always expect that arg1, if non-null, is of type connection
413 * (from which we can derive fconn), that arg2, if non-null, is of type fstrm,
414 * and that arg3, if non-null, is a htx for rx/tx headers.
415 */
416static void fcgi_trace(enum trace_level level, uint64_t mask, const struct trace_source *src,
417 const struct ist where, const struct ist func,
418 const void *a1, const void *a2, const void *a3, const void *a4)
419{
420 const struct connection *conn = a1;
421 const struct fcgi_conn *fconn = conn ? conn->ctx : NULL((void*)0);
422 const struct fcgi_strm *fstrm = a2;
423 const struct htx *htx = a3;
424 const size_t *val = a4;
425
426 if (!fconn)
427 fconn = (fstrm ? fstrm->fconn : NULL((void*)0));
428
429 if (!fconn || src->verbosity < FCGI_VERB_CLEAN1)
430 return;
431
432 /* Display the response state if fstrm is defined */
433 if (fstrm)
434 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " [rsp:%s]", h1m_state_str(fstrm->h1m.state));
435
436 if (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_CLEAN1)
437 return;
438
439 /* Display the value to the 4th argument (level > STATE) */
440 if (src->level > TRACE_LEVEL_STATE && val)
441 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " - VAL=%lu", (long)*val);
442
443 /* Display status-line if possible (verbosity > MINIMAL) */
444 if (src->verbosity > FCGI_VERB_MINIMAL2 && htx && htx_nbblks(htx)) {
445 const struct htx_blk *blk = htx_get_head_blk(htx);
446 const struct htx_sl *sl = htx_get_blk_ptr(htx, blk);
447 enum htx_blk_type type = htx_get_blk_type(blk);
448
449 if (type == HTX_BLK_REQ_SL || type == HTX_BLK_RES_SL)
450 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " - \"%.*s %.*s %.*s\"",
451 HTX_SL_P1_LEN(sl)((sl)->len[0]), HTX_SL_P1_PTR(sl)((sl)->l),
452 HTX_SL_P2_LEN(sl)((sl)->len[1]), HTX_SL_P2_PTR(sl)(((sl)->l) + ((sl)->len[0])),
453 HTX_SL_P3_LEN(sl)((sl)->len[2]), HTX_SL_P3_PTR(sl)((((sl)->l) + ((sl)->len[0])) + ((sl)->len[1])));
454 }
455
456 /* Display fconn info and, if defined, fstrm info */
457 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " - fconn=%p(%s,0x%08x)", fconn, fconn_st_to_str(fconn->state), fconn->flags);
458 if (fstrm)
459 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " fstrm=%p(%d,%s,0x%08x)", fstrm, fstrm->id, fstrm_st_to_str(fstrm->state), fstrm->flags);
460
461 if (!fstrm || fstrm->id <= 0)
462 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " dsi=%d", fconn->dsi);
463 if (fconn->dsi >= 0 && (mask & FCGI_EV_RX_FHDR(1ULL << 7)))
464 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " drt=%s", fcgi_rt_str(fconn->drt));
465
466 if (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_MINIMAL2)
467 return;
468
469 /* Display mbuf and dbuf info (level > USER & verbosity > SIMPLE) */
470 if (src->level > TRACE_LEVEL_USER) {
471 if (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_COMPLETE5 ||
472 (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_ADVANCED4 && (mask & (FCGI_EV_FCONN_RECV(1ULL << 1)|FCGI_EV_RX_RECORD(1ULL << 8)))))
473 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " dbuf=%u@%p+%u/%u",
474 (unsigned int)b_data(&fconn->dbuf), b_orig(&fconn->dbuf),
475 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(&fconn->dbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(&fconn->dbuf));
476 if (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_COMPLETE5 ||
477 (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_ADVANCED4 && (mask & (FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND(1ULL << 2)|FCGI_EV_TX_RECORD(1ULL << 14))))) {
478 struct buffer *hmbuf = br_head((struct buffer *)fconn->mbuf);
479 struct buffer *tmbuf = br_tail((struct buffer *)fconn->mbuf);
480
481 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " .mbuf=[%u..%u|%u],h=[%u@%p+%u/%u],t=[%u@%p+%u/%u]",
482 br_head_idx(fconn->mbuf), br_tail_idx(fconn->mbuf), br_size(fconn->mbuf),
483 (unsigned int)b_data(hmbuf), b_orig(hmbuf),
484 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(hmbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(hmbuf),
485 (unsigned int)b_data(tmbuf), b_orig(tmbuf),
486 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(tmbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(tmbuf));
487 }
488
489 if (fstrm && (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_COMPLETE5 ||
490 (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_ADVANCED4 && (mask & (FCGI_EV_STRM_RECV(1ULL << 31)|FCGI_EV_RSP_DATA(1ULL << 21))))))
491 chunk_appendf(&trace_buf, " rxbuf=%u@%p+%u/%u",
492 (unsigned int)b_data(&fstrm->rxbuf), b_orig(&fstrm->rxbuf),
493 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(&fstrm->rxbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(&fstrm->rxbuf));
494 }
495
496 /* Display htx info if defined (level > USER) */
497 if (src->level > TRACE_LEVEL_USER && htx) {
498 int full = 0;
499
500 /* Full htx info (level > STATE && verbosity > SIMPLE) */
501 if (src->level > TRACE_LEVEL_STATE) {
502 if (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_COMPLETE5)
503 full = 1;
504 else if (src->verbosity == FCGI_VERB_ADVANCED4 && (mask & (FCGI_EV_RSP_HDRS(1ULL << 23)|FCGI_EV_TX_PARAMS(1ULL << 18))))
505 full = 1;
506 }
507
508 chunk_memcat(&trace_buf, "\n\t", 2);
509 htx_dump(&trace_buf, htx, full);
510 }
511}
512
513/*****************************************************/
514/* functions below are for dynamic buffer management */
515/*****************************************************/
516
517/* Indicates whether or not the we may call the fcgi_recv() function to attempt
518 * to receive data into the buffer and/or demux pending data. The condition is
519 * a bit complex due to some API limits for now. The rules are the following :
520 * - if an error or a shutdown was detected on the connection and the buffer
521 * is empty, we must not attempt to receive
522 * - if the demux buf failed to be allocated, we must not try to receive and
523 * we know there is nothing pending
524 * - if no flag indicates a blocking condition, we may attempt to receive,
525 * regardless of whether the demux buffer is full or not, so that only
526 * de demux part decides whether or not to block. This is needed because
527 * the connection API indeed prevents us from re-enabling receipt that is
528 * already enabled in a polled state, so we must always immediately stop
529 * as soon as the demux can't proceed so as never to hit an end of read
530 * with data pending in the buffers.
531 * - otherwise must may not attempt
532 */
533static inline int fcgi_recv_allowed(const struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
534{
535 if (b_data(&fconn->dbuf) == 0 &&
536 (fconn->state == FCGI_CS_CLOSED ||
537 fconn->conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR ||
538 conn_xprt_read0_pending(fconn->conn)))
539 return 0;
540
541 if (!(fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_DEM_DALLOC0x00000004) &&
542 !(fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_DEM_BLOCK_ANY0x000000F0))
543 return 1;
544
545 return 0;
546}
547
548/* Restarts reading on the connection if it was not enabled */
549static inline void fcgi_conn_restart_reading(const struct fcgi_conn *fconn, int consider_buffer)
550{
551 if (!fcgi_recv_allowed(fconn))
552 return;
553 if ((!consider_buffer || !b_data(&fconn->dbuf)) &&
554 (fconn->wait_event.events & SUB_RETRY_RECV))
555 return;
556 tasklet_wakeup(fconn->wait_event.tasklet);
557}
558
559
560/* Tries to grab a buffer and to re-enable processing on mux <target>. The
561 * fcgi_conn flags are used to figure what buffer was requested. It returns 1 if
562 * the allocation succeeds, in which case the connection is woken up, or 0 if
563 * it's impossible to wake up and we prefer to be woken up later.
564 */
565static int fcgi_buf_available(void *target)
566{
567 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = target;
568 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm;
569
570 if ((fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_DEM_DALLOC0x00000004) && b_alloc_margin(&fconn->dbuf, 0)) {
571 TRACE_STATE("unblocking fconn, dbuf allocated", FCGI_EV_FCONN_RECV|FCGI_EV_FCONN_BLK|FCGI_EV_FCONN_WAKE, fconn->conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_STATE, ((1ULL << 1)|(1ULL << 3)
|(1ULL << 4)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *)
("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "571"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len =
__builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "571") ? ((void *)
"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "571" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }), ((void*)0), fconn->conn,((void*)0),((void
*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (void *)("unblocking fconn, dbuf allocated"
); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("unblocking fconn, dbuf allocated"
) ? ((void *)"unblocking fconn, dbuf allocated" == (void *)0)
? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for
(__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
572 fconn->flags &= ~FCGI_CF_DEM_DALLOC0x00000004;
573 fcgi_conn_restart_reading(fconn, 1);
574 return 1;
575 }
576
577 if ((fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001) && b_alloc_margin(br_tail(fconn->mbuf), 0)) {
578 TRACE_STATE("unblocking fconn, mbuf allocated", FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND|FCGI_EV_FCONN_BLK|FCGI_EV_FCONN_WAKE, fconn->conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_STATE, ((1ULL << 2)|(1ULL << 3)
|(1ULL << 4)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *)
("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "578"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len =
__builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "578") ? ((void *)
"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "578" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }), ((void*)0), fconn->conn,((void*)0),((void
*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (void *)("unblocking fconn, mbuf allocated"
); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("unblocking fconn, mbuf allocated"
) ? ((void *)"unblocking fconn, mbuf allocated" == (void *)0)
? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for
(__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
579 fconn->flags &= ~FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001;
580 if (fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_DEM_MROOM0x00000010) {
581 fconn->flags &= ~FCGI_CF_DEM_MROOM0x00000010;
582 fcgi_conn_restart_reading(fconn, 1);
583 }
584 return 1;
585 }
586
587 if ((fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_DEM_SALLOC0x00000020) &&
588 (fstrm = fcgi_conn_st_by_id(fconn, fconn->dsi)) && fstrm->cs &&
589 b_alloc_margin(&fstrm->rxbuf, 0)) {
590 TRACE_STATE("unblocking fstrm, rxbuf allocated", FCGI_EV_STRM_RECV|FCGI_EV_FSTRM_BLK|FCGI_EV_STRM_WAKE, fconn->conn, fstrm)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_STATE, ((1ULL << 31)|(1ULL << 27
)|(1ULL << 34)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *
)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "590"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len
= __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "590") ? ((void *
)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "590" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }), ((void*)0), fconn->conn,fstrm,((void*)0)
,((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (void *)("unblocking fstrm, rxbuf allocated"
); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("unblocking fstrm, rxbuf allocated"
) ? ((void *)"unblocking fstrm, rxbuf allocated" == (void *)0
) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for
(__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
591 fconn->flags &= ~FCGI_CF_DEM_SALLOC0x00000020;
592 fcgi_conn_restart_reading(fconn, 1);
593 fcgi_strm_notify_recv(fstrm);
594 return 1;
595 }
596
597 return 0;
598}

600static inline struct buffer *fcgi_get_buf(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, struct buffer *bptr)
601{
602 struct buffer *buf = NULL((void*)0);
603
604 if (likely(!MT_LIST_ADDED(&fconn->buf_wait.list))(__builtin_expect((!((&fconn->buf_wait.list)->next !=
(&fconn->buf_wait.list))) != 0, 1)) &&
605 unlikely((buf = b_alloc_margin(bptr, 0)) == NULL)(__builtin_expect(((buf = b_alloc_margin(bptr, 0)) == ((void*
)0)) != 0, 0))) {
606 fconn->buf_wait.target = fconn;
607 fconn->buf_wait.wakeup_cb = fcgi_buf_available;
608 MT_LIST_ADDQ(&buffer_wq, &fconn->buf_wait.list)({ int _ret = 0; struct mt_list *lh = (&buffer_wq), *el =
(&fconn->buf_wait.list); while (1) { struct mt_list *
n; struct mt_list *p; p = __atomic_exchange_n(&(lh)->prev
, ((struct mt_list *)1), 0); if (p == ((struct mt_list *)1)) continue
; n = __atomic_exchange_n(&p->next, ((struct mt_list *
)1), 0); if (n == ((struct mt_list *)1)) { (lh)->prev = p;
__ha_barrier_store(); continue; } if ((el)->next != (el) ||
(el)->prev != (el)) { p->next = n; (lh)->prev = p; break
; } (el)->next = n; (el)->prev = p; __ha_barrier_store(
); p->next = (el); __ha_barrier_store(); n->prev = (el)
; __ha_barrier_store(); _ret = 1; break; } (_ret); });
609 }
610 return buf;
611}
612
613static inline void fcgi_release_buf(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, struct buffer *bptr)
614{
615 if (bptr->size) {
616 b_free(bptr);
617 offer_buffers(NULL((void*)0), tasks_run_queue);
618 }
619}
620
621static inline void fcgi_release_mbuf(struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
622{
623 struct buffer *buf;
624 unsigned int count = 0;
625
626 while (b_size(buf = br_head_pick(fconn->mbuf))) {
627 b_free(buf);
628 count++;
629 }
630 if (count)
631 offer_buffers(NULL((void*)0), tasks_run_queue);
632}
633
634/* Returns the number of allocatable outgoing streams for the connection taking
635 * the number reserved streams into account.
636 */
637static inline int fcgi_streams_left(const struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
638{
639 int ret;
640
641 ret = (unsigned int)(0x7FFF - fconn->max_id) - fconn->nb_reserved - 1;
642 if (ret < 0)
643 ret = 0;
644 return ret;
645}
646
647/* Returns the number of streams in use on a connection to figure if it's
648 * idle or not. We check nb_cs and not nb_streams as the caller will want
649 * to know if it was the last one after a detach().
650 */
651static int fcgi_used_streams(struct connection *conn)
652{
653 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = conn->ctx;
654
655 return fconn->nb_cs;
656}
657
658/* Returns the number of concurrent streams available on the connection */
659static int fcgi_avail_streams(struct connection *conn)
660{
661 struct server *srv = objt_server(conn->target);
662 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = conn->ctx;
663 int ret1, ret2;
664
665 /* Don't open new stream if the connection is closed */
666 if (fconn->state == FCGI_CS_CLOSED)
667 return 0;
668
669 /* May be negative if this setting has changed */
670 ret1 = (fconn->streams_limit - fconn->nb_streams);
671
672 /* we must also consider the limit imposed by stream IDs */
673 ret2 = fcgi_streams_left(fconn);
674 ret1 = MIN(ret1, ret2)(((ret1)<(ret2))?(ret1):(ret2));
675 if (ret1 > 0 && srv && srv->max_reuse >= 0) {
676 ret2 = ((fconn->stream_cnt <= srv->max_reuse) ? srv->max_reuse - fconn->stream_cnt + 1: 0);
677 ret1 = MIN(ret1, ret2)(((ret1)<(ret2))?(ret1):(ret2));
678 }
679 return ret1;
680}
681
682/*****************************************************************/
683/* functions below are dedicated to the mux setup and management */
684/*****************************************************************/
685
686/* Initializes the mux once it's attached. Only outgoing connections are
687 * supported. So the context is already initialized before installing the
688 * mux. <input> is always used as Input buffer and may contain data. It is the
689 * caller responsibility to not reuse it anymore. Returns < 0 on error.
690 */
691static int fcgi_init(struct connection *conn, struct proxy *px, struct session *sess,
692 struct buffer *input)
693{
694 struct fcgi_conn *fconn;
695 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm;
696 struct fcgi_app *app = get_px_fcgi_app(px);
697 struct task *t = NULL((void*)0);
698 void *conn_ctx = conn->ctx;
699
700 TRACE_ENTER(FCGI_EV_FSTRM_NEW)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 26)), &trace_fcgi
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "700"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "700") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "700" == (void *)
0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for
(__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, ((void*
)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x
= (void *)("entering"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("entering") ? ((void *)"entering" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }));
701
702 if (!app)
703 goto fail_conn;
704
705 fconn = pool_alloc(pool_head_fcgi_conn);
706 if (!fconn)
707 goto fail_conn;
708
709 fconn->shut_timeout = fconn->timeout = px->timeout.server;
710 if (tick_isset(px->timeout.serverfin))
711 fconn->shut_timeout = px->timeout.serverfin;
712
713 fconn->flags = FCGI_CF_NONE0x00000000;
714
715 /* Retrieve useful info from the FCGI app */
716 if (app->flags & FCGI_APP_FL_KEEP_CONN0x00000001)
717 fconn->flags |= FCGI_CF_KEEP_CONN0x00001000;
718 if (app->flags & FCGI_APP_FL_GET_VALUES0x00000002)
719 fconn->flags |= FCGI_CF_GET_VALUES0x00002000;
720 if (app->flags & FCGI_APP_FL_MPXS_CONNS0x00000004)
721 fconn->flags |= FCGI_CF_MPXS_CONNS0x00000100;
722
723 fconn->proxy = px;
724 fconn->app = app;
725 fconn->task = NULL((void*)0);
726 if (tick_isset(fconn->timeout)) {
727 t = task_new(tid_bit);
728 if (!t)
729 goto fail;
730
731 fconn->task = t;
732 t->process = fcgi_timeout_task;
733 t->context = fconn;
734 t->expire = tick_add(now_ms, fconn->timeout);
735 }
736
737 fconn->wait_event.tasklet = tasklet_new();
738 if (!fconn->wait_event.tasklet)
739 goto fail;

793/* Returns the next allocatable outgoing stream ID for the FCGI connection, or
794 * -1 if no more is allocatable.
795 */
796static inline int32_t fcgi_conn_get_next_sid(const struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
797{
798 int32_t id = (fconn->max_id + 1) | 1;
799
800 if ((id & 0x80000000U))
801 id = -1;
802 return id;
803}

810 if (id == 0)

18
←

815

fcgi_strm *)0)->by_id)));

871/* Returns true if the FCGI connection must be release */
872static inline int fcgi_conn_is_dead(struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
873{
874 if (eb_is_empty(&fconn->streams_by_id) && /* don't close if streams exist */
875 (!(fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_KEEP_CONN0x00001000) || /* don't keep the connection alive */
876 (fconn->conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR) || /* errors close immediately */
877 (fconn->state == FCGI_CS_CLOSED && !fconn->task) ||/* a timeout stroke earlier */
878 (!(fconn->conn->owner)) || /* Nobody's left to take care of the connection, drop it now */
879 (!br_data(fconn->mbuf) && /* mux buffer empty, also process clean events below */
880 conn_xprt_read0_pending(fconn->conn))))
881 return 1;
882 return 0;
883}

956/* Writes the 16-bit record size <len> at address <record> */
957static inline void fcgi_set_record_size(void *record, uint16_t len)
958{
959 uint8_t *out = (record + 4);
960
961 *out = (len >> 8);
962 *(out + 1) = (len & 0xff);
963}
964
965/* Writes the 16-bit stream id <id> at address <record> */
966static inline void fcgi_set_record_id(void *record, uint16_t id)
967{
968 uint8_t *out = (record + 2);
969
970 *out = (id >> 8);
971 *(out + 1) = (id & 0xff);
972}

974/* Marks a FCGI stream as CLOSED and decrement the number of active streams for
975 * its connection if the stream was not yet closed. Please use this exclusively
976 * before closing a stream to ensure stream count is well maintained.
977 */
978static inline void fcgi_strm_close(struct fcgi_strm *fstrm)
979{

fconn->conn,fstrm,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char

) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));

1116/* Wakes a specific stream and assign its conn_stream some CS_FL_* flags among

1159/* Wakes unassigned streams (ID == 0) attached to the connection. */
1160static void fcgi_wake_unassigned_streams(struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
1161{
1162 struct eb32_node *node;
1163 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm;
1164
1165 node = eb32_lookup(&fconn->streams_by_id, 0);
1166 while (node) {
1167 fstrm = container_of(node, struct fcgi_strm, by_id)((struct fcgi_strm *)(((void *)(node)) - ((long)&((struct
fcgi_strm *)0)->by_id)));
1168 if (fstrm->id > 0)
1169 break;
1170 node = eb32_next(node);
1171 fcgi_strm_wake_one_stream(fstrm);
1172 }
1173}
1174
1175/* Wakes the streams attached to the connection, whose id is greater than <last>
1176 * or unassigned.
1177 */
1178static void fcgi_wake_some_streams(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, int last)
1179{
1180 struct eb32_node *node;
1181 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm;
1182
1183 TRACE_ENTER(FCGI_EV_STRM_WAKE, fconn->conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 34)), &trace_fcgi
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1183"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "1183") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1183" == (void *
)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x)
for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, fconn
->conn,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char
*__x = (void *)("entering"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len =
__builtin_constant_p("entering") ? ((void *)"entering" == (void
*)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x
) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
1184
1185 /* Wake all streams with ID > last */
1186 node = eb32_lookup_ge(&fconn->streams_by_id, last + 1);
1187 while (node) {
1188 fstrm = container_of(node, struct fcgi_strm, by_id)((struct fcgi_strm *)(((void *)(node)) - ((long)&((struct
fcgi_strm *)0)->by_id)));
1189 node = eb32_next(node);
1190 fcgi_strm_wake_one_stream(fstrm);
1191 }
1192 fcgi_wake_unassigned_streams(fconn);
1193
1194 TRACE_LEAVE(FCGI_EV_STRM_WAKE, fconn->conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 34)), &trace_fcgi
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1194"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "1194") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1194" == (void *
)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x)
for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, fconn
->conn,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char
*__x = (void *)("leaving"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len =
__builtin_constant_p("leaving") ? ((void *)"leaving" == (void
*)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x
) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
1195}
1196
1197static int fcgi_set_default_param(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, struct fcgi_strm *fstrm,
1198 struct htx *htx, struct htx_sl *sl,
1199 struct fcgi_strm_params *params)
1200{
1201 struct connection *cli_conn = objt_conn(fstrm->sess->origin);
1202 struct ist p;
1203
1204 if (!sl)
1205 goto error;
1206
1207 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_DOC_ROOT0x00000002))
1208 params->docroot = fconn->app->docroot;
1209
1210 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_REQ_METH0x00000020)) {
1211 p = htx_sl_req_meth(sl);
1212 params->meth = ist2(b_tail(params->p), p.len);
1213 chunk_memcat(params->p, p.ptr, p.len);
1214 }
1215 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_REQ_URI0x00000010)) {
1216 p = htx_sl_req_uri(sl);
1217 params->uri = ist2(b_tail(params->p), p.len);
1218 chunk_memcat(params->p, p.ptr, p.len);
1219 }
1220 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_SRV_PROTO0x00000100)) {
1221 p = htx_sl_req_vsn(sl);
1222 params->vsn = ist2(b_tail(params->p), p.len);
1223 chunk_memcat(params->p, p.ptr, p.len);
1224 }
1225 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_SRV_PORT0x00000080)) {
1226 char *end;
1227 int port = 0;
1228 if (conn_get_dst(cli_conn))
1229 port = get_host_port(cli_conn->dst);
1230 end = ultoa_o(port, b_tail(params->p), b_room(params->p));
1231 if (!end)
1232 goto error;
1233 params->srv_port = ist2(b_tail(params->p), end - b_tail(params->p));
1234 params->p->data += params->srv_port.len;
1235 }
1236 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_SRV_NAME0x00000200)) {
1237 /* If no Host header found, use the server address to fill
1238 * srv_name */
1239 if (!istlen(params->srv_name)) {
1240 char *ptr = NULL((void*)0);
1241
1242 if (conn_get_dst(cli_conn))
1243 if (addr_to_str(cli_conn->dst, b_tail(params->p), b_room(params->p)) != -1)
1244 ptr = b_tail(params->p);
1245 if (ptr) {
1246 params->srv_name = ist2(ptr, strlen(ptr));
1247 params->p->data += params->srv_name.len;
1248 }
1249 }
1250 }
1251 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_REM_ADDR0x00000400)) {
1252 char *ptr = NULL((void*)0);
1253
1254 if (conn_get_src(cli_conn))
1255 if (addr_to_str(cli_conn->src, b_tail(params->p), b_room(params->p)) != -1)
1256 ptr = b_tail(params->p);
1257 if (ptr) {
1258 params->rem_addr = ist2(ptr, strlen(ptr));
1259 params->p->data += params->rem_addr.len;
1260 }
1261 }
1262 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_REM_PORT0x00000800)) {
1263 char *end;
1264 int port = 0;
1265 if (conn_get_src(cli_conn))
1266 port = get_host_port(cli_conn->src);
1267 end = ultoa_o(port, b_tail(params->p), b_room(params->p));
1268 if (!end)
1269 goto error;
1270 params->rem_port = ist2(b_tail(params->p), end - b_tail(params->p));
1271 params->p->data += params->rem_port.len;
1272 }
1273 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_CONT_LEN0x00004000)) {
1274 struct htx_blk *blk;
1275 enum htx_blk_type type;
1276 char *end;
1277 size_t len = 0;
1278
1279 for (blk = htx_get_head_blk(htx); blk; blk = htx_get_next_blk(htx, blk)) {
1280 type = htx_get_blk_type(blk);
1281
1282 if (type == HTX_BLK_EOM || type == HTX_BLK_TLR || type == HTX_BLK_EOT)
1283 break;
1284 if (type == HTX_BLK_DATA)
1285 len += htx_get_blksz(blk);
1286 }
1287 end = ultoa_o(len, b_tail(params->p), b_room(params->p));
1288 if (!end)
1289 goto error;
1290 params->cont_len = ist2(b_tail(params->p), end - b_tail(params->p));
1291 params->p->data += params->cont_len.len;
1292 }
1293#ifdef USE_OPENSSL1
1294 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_HTTPS0x00008000)) {
1295 params->https = ssl_sock_is_ssl(cli_conn);
1296 }
1297#endif
1298 if ((params->mask & FCGI_SP_URI_MASK(0x00000004|0x00000008|0x00000040)) != FCGI_SP_URI_MASK(0x00000004|0x00000008|0x00000040)) {
1299 /* one of scriptname, pathinfo or query_string is no set */
1300 struct ist path = http_get_path(params->uri);
1301 int len;
1302
1303 /* Decode the path. it must first be copied to keep the URI
1304 * untouched.
1305 */
1306 chunk_memcat(params->p, path.ptr, path.len);
1307 path.ptr = b_tail(params->p) - path.len;
1308 path.ptr[path.len] = '\0';
1309 len = url_decode(path.ptr);
1310 if (len < 0)
1311 goto error;
1312 path.len = len;
1313
1314 /* No scrit_name set but no valid path ==> error */
1315 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_SCRIPT_NAME0x00000004) && !istlen(path))
1316 goto error;
1317
1318 /* Find limit between the path and the query-string */
1319 for (len = 0; len < path.len && *(path.ptr + len) != '?'; len++);
1320
1321 /* If there is a query-string, Set it if not already set */
1322 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_REQ_QS0x00000040) && len < path.len)
1323 params->qs = ist2(path.ptr+len+1, path.len-len-1);
1324
1325 /* If the script_name is set, don't try to deduce the path_info
1326 * too. The opposite is not true.
1327 */
1328 if (params->mask & FCGI_SP_SCRIPT_NAME0x00000004) {
1329 params->mask |= FCGI_SP_PATH_INFO0x00000008;
1330 goto end;
1331 }
1332
1333 /* script_name not set, preset it with the path for now */
1334 params->scriptname = ist2(path.ptr, len);
1335
1336 /* If there is no regex to match the pathinfo, just to the last
1337 * part and see if the index must be used.
1338 */
1339 if (!fconn->app->pathinfo_re)
1340 goto check_index;
1341
1342 /* If some special characters are found in the decoded path (\n
1343 * or \0), the PATH_INFO regex cannot match. This is theorically
1344 * valid, but probably unexpected, to have such characters. So,
1345 * to avoid any surprises, an error is triggered in this
1346 * case.
1347 */
1348 if (istchr(path, '\n') || istchr(path, '\0'))
1349 goto error;
1350
1351 /* The regex does not match, just to the last part and see if
1352 * the index must be used.
1353 */
1354 if (!regex_exec_match2(fconn->app->pathinfo_re, path.ptr, len, MAX_MATCH10, pmatch, 0))
1355 goto check_index;
1356
1357 /* We must have at least 1 capture for the script name,
1358 * otherwise we do nothing and jump to the last part.
1359 */
1360 if (pmatch[1].rm_so == -1 || pmatch[1].rm_eo == -1)
1361 goto check_index;
1362
1363 /* Finally we can set the script_name and the path_info. The
1364 * path_info is set if not already defined, and if it was
1365 * captured
1366 */
1367 params->scriptname = ist2(path.ptr + pmatch[1].rm_so, pmatch[1].rm_eo - pmatch[1].rm_so);
1368 if (!(params->mask & FCGI_SP_PATH_INFO0x00000008) && (pmatch[2].rm_so == -1 || pmatch[2].rm_eo == -1))
1369 params->pathinfo = ist2(path.ptr + pmatch[2].rm_so, pmatch[2].rm_eo - pmatch[2].rm_so);
1370
1371 check_index:
1372 len = params->scriptname.len;
1373 /* the script_name if finished by a '/' so we can add the index
1374 * part, if any.
1375 */
1376 if (istlen(fconn->app->index) && params->scriptname.ptr[len-1] == '/') {
1377 struct ist sn = params->scriptname;
1378
1379 params->scriptname = ist2(b_tail(params->p), len+fconn->app->index.len);
1380 chunk_memcat(params->p, sn.ptr, sn.len);
1381 chunk_memcat(params->p, fconn->app->index.ptr, fconn->app->index.len);
1382 }
1383 }
1384
1385 end:
1386 return 1;
1387 error:
1388 return 0;
1389}
1390
1391static int fcgi_encode_default_param(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, struct fcgi_strm *fstrm,
1392 struct fcgi_strm_params *params, struct buffer *outbuf, int flag)
1393{
1394 struct fcgi_param p;
1395
1396 if (params->mask & flag)
1397 return 1;
1398
1399 chunk_reset(&trash);
1400
1401 switch (flag) {
1402 case FCGI_SP_CGI_GATEWAY0x00000001:
1403 p.n = ist("GATEWAY_INTERFACE")({ char *__x = (void *)("GATEWAY_INTERFACE"); (struct ist){ .
ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("GATEWAY_INTERFACE") ?
((void *)"GATEWAY_INTERFACE" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; });
1404 p.v = ist("CGI/1.1")({ char *__x = (void *)("CGI/1.1"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x,
.len = __builtin_constant_p("CGI/1.1") ? ((void *)"CGI/1.1" ==
(void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if
(__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1405 goto encode;
1406 case FCGI_SP_DOC_ROOT0x00000002:
1407 p.n = ist("DOCUMENT_ROOT")({ char *__x = (void *)("DOCUMENT_ROOT"); (struct ist){ .ptr =
__x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("DOCUMENT_ROOT") ? ((void *
)"DOCUMENT_ROOT" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : (
{ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }
) }; });
1408 p.v = params->docroot;
1409 goto encode;
1410 case FCGI_SP_SCRIPT_NAME0x00000004:
1411 p.n = ist("SCRIPT_NAME")({ char *__x = (void *)("SCRIPT_NAME"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("SCRIPT_NAME") ? ((void *)"SCRIPT_NAME"
== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1412 p.v = params->scriptname;
1413 goto encode;
1414 case FCGI_SP_PATH_INFO0x00000008:
1415 p.n = ist("PATH_INFO")({ char *__x = (void *)("PATH_INFO"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("PATH_INFO") ? ((void *)"PATH_INFO"
== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1416 p.v = params->pathinfo;
1417 goto encode;
1418 case FCGI_SP_REQ_URI0x00000010:
1419 p.n = ist("REQUEST_URI")({ char *__x = (void *)("REQUEST_URI"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("REQUEST_URI") ? ((void *)"REQUEST_URI"
== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1420 p.v = params->uri;
1421 goto encode;
1422 case FCGI_SP_REQ_METH0x00000020:
1423 p.n = ist("REQUEST_METHOD")({ char *__x = (void *)("REQUEST_METHOD"); (struct ist){ .ptr
= __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("REQUEST_METHOD") ? ((void
*)"REQUEST_METHOD" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x)
: ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l
; }) }; });
1424 p.v = params->meth;
1425 goto encode;
1426 case FCGI_SP_REQ_QS0x00000040:
1427 p.n = ist("QUERY_STRING")({ char *__x = (void *)("QUERY_STRING"); (struct ist){ .ptr =
__x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("QUERY_STRING") ? ((void *)
"QUERY_STRING" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({
size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; })
}; });
1428 p.v = params->qs;
1429 goto encode;
1430 case FCGI_SP_SRV_NAME0x00000200:
1431 p.n = ist("SERVER_NAME")({ char *__x = (void *)("SERVER_NAME"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("SERVER_NAME") ? ((void *)"SERVER_NAME"
== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1432 p.v = params->srv_name;
1433 goto encode;

1435 p.n = ist("SERVER_PORT")({ char *__x = (void *)("SERVER_PORT"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x

== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });

1437 goto encode;

1439 p.n = ist("SERVER_PROTOCOL")({ char *__x = (void *)("SERVER_PROTOCOL"); (struct ist){ .ptr
= __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("SERVER_PROTOCOL") ? ((void
*)"SERVER_PROTOCOL" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x
) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l
; }) }; });
1440 p.v = params->vsn;
1441 goto encode;
1442 case FCGI_SP_REM_ADDR0x00000400:
1443 p.n = ist("REMOTE_ADDR")({ char *__x = (void *)("REMOTE_ADDR"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("REMOTE_ADDR") ? ((void *)"REMOTE_ADDR"
== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1444 p.v = params->rem_addr;
1445 goto encode;
1446 case FCGI_SP_REM_PORT0x00000800:
1447 p.n = ist("REMOTE_PORT")({ char *__x = (void *)("REMOTE_PORT"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("REMOTE_PORT") ? ((void *)"REMOTE_PORT"
== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0
; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1448 p.v = params->rem_port;
1449 goto encode;
1450 case FCGI_SP_SCRIPT_FILE0x00001000:
1451 p.n = ist("SCRIPT_FILENAME")({ char *__x = (void *)("SCRIPT_FILENAME"); (struct ist){ .ptr
= __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("SCRIPT_FILENAME") ? ((void
*)"SCRIPT_FILENAME" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x
) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l
; }) }; });
1452 chunk_memcat(&trash, params->docroot.ptr, params->docroot.len);
1453 chunk_memcat(&trash, params->scriptname.ptr, params->scriptname.len);
1454 p.v = ist2(b_head(&trash), b_data(&trash));
1455 goto encode;
1456 case FCGI_SP_PATH_TRANS0x00002000:
1457 if (!istlen(params->pathinfo))
1458 goto skip;
1459 p.n = ist("PATH_TRANSLATED")({ char *__x = (void *)("PATH_TRANSLATED"); (struct ist){ .ptr
= __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("PATH_TRANSLATED") ? ((void
*)"PATH_TRANSLATED" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x
) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l
; }) }; });
1460 chunk_memcat(&trash, params->docroot.ptr, params->docroot.len);
1461 chunk_memcat(&trash, params->pathinfo.ptr, params->pathinfo.len);
1462 p.v = ist2(b_head(&trash), b_data(&trash));
1463 goto encode;
1464 case FCGI_SP_CONT_LEN0x00004000:
1465 p.n = ist("CONTENT_LENGTH")({ char *__x = (void *)("CONTENT_LENGTH"); (struct ist){ .ptr
= __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("CONTENT_LENGTH") ? ((void
*)"CONTENT_LENGTH" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x)
: ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l
; }) }; });
1466 p.v = params->cont_len;
1467 goto encode;
1468 case FCGI_SP_HTTPS0x00008000:
1469 if (!params->https)
1470 goto skip;
1471 p.n = ist("HTTPS")({ char *__x = (void *)("HTTPS"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .
len = __builtin_constant_p("HTTPS") ? ((void *)"HTTPS" == (void
*)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x
) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1472 p.v = ist("on")({ char *__x = (void *)("on"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len
= __builtin_constant_p("on") ? ((void *)"on" == (void *)0) ?
0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (
__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; });
1473 goto encode;
1474 default:
1475 goto skip;
1476 }
1477
1478 encode:
1479 if (!istlen(p.v))
1480 goto skip;
1481 if (!fcgi_encode_param(outbuf, &p))
1482 return 0;
1483 skip:
1484 params->mask |= flag;
1485 return 1;
1486}
1487
1488/* Sends a GET_VALUES record. Returns > 0 on success, 0 if it couldn't do
1489 * anything. It is highly unexpected, but if the record is larger than a buffer
1490 * and cannot be encoded in one time, an error is triggered and the connection is
1491 * closed. GET_VALUES record cannot be split.
1492 */
1493static int fcgi_conn_send_get_values(struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
1494{
1495 struct buffer outbuf;
1496 struct buffer *mbuf;
1497 struct fcgi_param max_reqs = { .n = ist("FCGI_MAX_REQS")({ char *__x = (void *)("FCGI_MAX_REQS"); (struct ist){ .ptr =
__x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("FCGI_MAX_REQS") ? ((void *
)"FCGI_MAX_REQS" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : (
{ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }
) }; }), .v = ist("")({ char *__x = (void *)(""); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len =
__builtin_constant_p("") ? ((void *)"" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; })};
1498 struct fcgi_param mpxs_conns = { .n = ist("FCGI_MPXS_CONNS")({ char *__x = (void *)("FCGI_MPXS_CONNS"); (struct ist){ .ptr
= __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("FCGI_MPXS_CONNS") ? ((void
*)"FCGI_MPXS_CONNS" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x
) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l
; }) }; }), .v = ist("")({ char *__x = (void *)(""); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len =
__builtin_constant_p("") ? ((void *)"" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; })};
1499 int ret = 0;
1500
1501 TRACE_ENTER(FCGI_EV_TX_RECORD|FCGI_EV_TX_GETVAL, fconn->conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 14)|(1ULL <<
17)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "1501"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1501") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":"
"1501" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t
__l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }),
__FUNCTION__, fconn->conn,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0
),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (void *)("entering"); (struct ist
){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("entering") ? ((void
*)"entering" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t
__l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
1502
1503 mbuf = br_tail(fconn->mbuf);
1504 retry:
1505 if (!fcgi_get_buf(fconn, mbuf)) {
1506 fconn->flags |= FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001;

1563/* Processes a GET_VALUES_RESULT record. Returns > 0 on success, 0 if it

1860/* Sends a PARAMS record. Returns > 0 on success, 0 if it couldn't do
1861 * anything. If there are too much K/V params to be encoded in a PARAMS record,
1862 * several records are sent. However, a K/V param cannot be split between 2
1863 * records.
1864 */
1865static size_t fcgi_strm_send_params(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, struct fcgi_strm *fstrm,
1866 struct htx *htx)
1867{
1868 struct buffer outbuf;
1869 struct buffer *mbuf;
1870 struct htx_blk *blk;
1871 struct htx_sl *sl = NULL((void*)0);
1872 struct fcgi_strm_params params;
1873 size_t total = 0;

18)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "1875"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1875") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":"
"1875" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t
__l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }),
__FUNCTION__, fconn->conn,fstrm,htx,((void*)0),((void*)0)
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("entering"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x

1876
1877 memset(&params, 0, sizeof(params));
1878 params.p = get_trash_chunk();
1879

1882 if (!fcgi_get_buf(fconn, mbuf)) {
1883 fconn->flags |= FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001;
1884 fstrm->flags |= FCGI_SF_BLK_MROOM0x00000020;
1885 TRACE_STATE("waiting for fconn mbuf ring allocation", FCGI_EV_TX_RECORD|FCGI_EV_FSTRM_BLK|FCGI_EV_FCONN_BLK, fconn->conn, fstrm)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_STATE, ((1ULL << 14)|(1ULL << 27
)|(1ULL << 3)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *
)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "1885"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len

2073/* Sends a STDIN record. Returns > 0 on success, 0 if it couldn't do
2074 * anything. STDIN records contain the request body.

2099 /* Perform some optimizations to reduce the number of buffer copies.
2100 * First, if the mux's buffer is empty and the htx area contains exactly
2101 * one data block of the same size as the requested count, and this
2102 * count fits within the record size, then it's possible to simply swap
2103 * the caller's buffer with the mux's output buffer and adjust offsets
2104 * and length to match the entire DATA HTX block in the middle. In this
2105 * case we perform a true zero-copy operation from end-to-end. This is
2106 * the situation that happens all the time with large files. Second, if
2107 * this is not possible, but the mux's output buffer is empty, we still
2108 * have an opportunity to avoid the copy to the intermediary buffer, by
2109 * making the intermediary buffer's area point to the output buffer's
2110 * area. In this case we want to skip the HTX header to make sure that
2111 * copies remain aligned and that this operation remains possible all
2112 * the time. This goes for headers, data blocks and any data extracted
2113 * from the HTX blocks.
2114 */
2115 blk = htx_get_head_blk(htx);
2116 if (!blk)
2117 goto end;
2118 type = htx_get_blk_type(blk);
2119 size = htx_get_blksz(blk);
2120 if (unlikely(size == count && htx_nbblks(htx) == 1 && type == HTX_BLK_DATA)(__builtin_expect((size == count && htx_nbblks(htx) ==
1 && type == HTX_BLK_DATA) != 0, 0))) {
2121 void *old_area = mbuf->area;
2122
2123 if (b_data(mbuf)) {
2124 /* Too bad there are data left there. We're willing to memcpy/memmove
2125 * up to 1/4 of the buffer, which means that it's OK to copy a large
2126 * record into a buffer containing few data if it needs to be realigned,
2127 * and that it's also OK to copy few data without realigning. Otherwise
2128 * we'll pretend the mbuf is full and wait for it to become empty.
2129 */
2130 if (size + 8 <= b_room(mbuf) &&
2131 (b_data(mbuf) <= b_size(mbuf) / 4 ||
2132 (size <= b_size(mbuf) / 4 && size + 8 <= b_contig_space(mbuf))))
2133 goto copy;
2134 goto full;
2135 }
2136
2137 TRACE_PROTO("sending stding data (zero-copy)", FCGI_EV_TX_RECORD|FCGI_EV_TX_STDIN, fconn->conn, fstrm, htx, (size_t[]){size})trace(TRACE_LEVEL_PROTO, ((1ULL << 14)|(1ULL << 19
)), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "2137"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p

__l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }),

2139 * record header there.

2145 memcpy(outbuf.area, "\x01\x05\x00\x00\x00\x00\x00\x00", 8);
2146 fcgi_set_record_id(outbuf.area, fstrm->id);
2147 fcgi_set_record_size(outbuf.area, size);

2151 buf->data = buf->head = 0;

2396 * anything. If the empty STDOUT record is not already received, this one marks

2761
2762/* Try to send data if possible.
2763 * The function returns 1 if data have been sent, otherwise zero.
2764 */
2765static int fcgi_send(struct fcgi_conn *fconn)
2766{
2767 struct connection *conn = fconn->conn;
2768 int done;
2769 int sent = 0;
2770
2771 TRACE_ENTER(FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND, conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 2)), &trace_fcgi
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2771"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "2771") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2771" == (void *
)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x)
for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, conn
,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (
void *)("entering"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("entering") ? ((void *)"entering" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }));
2772
2773 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR) {
2774 TRACE_DEVEL("leaving on connection error", FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND, conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 2)), &trace_fcgi
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2774"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "2774") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2774" == (void *
)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x)
for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, conn
,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (
void *)("leaving on connection error"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x
, .len = __builtin_constant_p("leaving on connection error") ?
((void *)"leaving on connection error" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }));
2775 return 1;
2776 }
2777
2778
2779 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_XPRT) {
2780 /* a handshake was requested */
2781 goto schedule;
2782 }
2783
2784 /* This loop is quite simple : it tries to fill as much as it can from
2785 * pending streams into the existing buffer until it's reportedly full
2786 * or the end of send requests is reached. Then it tries to send this
2787 * buffer's contents out, marks it not full if at least one byte could
2788 * be sent, and tries again.
2789 *
2790 * The snd_buf() function normally takes a "flags" argument which may
2791 * be made of a combination of CO_SFL_MSG_MORE to indicate that more
2792 * data immediately comes and CO_SFL_STREAMER to indicate that the
2793 * connection is streaming lots of data (used to increase TLS record
2794 * size at the expense of latency). The former can be sent any time
2795 * there's a buffer full flag, as it indicates at least one stream
2796 * attempted to send and failed so there are pending data. An
2797 * alternative would be to set it as long as there's an active stream
2798 * but that would be problematic for ACKs until we have an absolute
2799 * guarantee that all waiters have at least one byte to send. The
2800 * latter should possibly not be set for now.
2801 */
2802
2803 done = 0;
2804 while (!done) {
2805 unsigned int flags = 0;
2806 unsigned int released = 0;
2807 struct buffer *buf;
2808
2809 /* fill as much as we can into the current buffer */
2810 while (((fconn->flags & (FCGI_CF_MUX_MFULL0x00000002|FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001)) == 0) && !done)
2811 done = fcgi_process_mux(fconn);
2812
2813 if (fconn->flags & FCGI_CF_MUX_MALLOC0x00000001)
2814 done = 1; // we won't go further without extra buffers
2815
2816 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_ERROR)
2817 break;
2818
2819 if (fconn->flags & (FCGI_CF_MUX_MFULL0x00000002 | FCGI_CF_DEM_MROOM0x00000010))
2820 flags |= CO_SFL_MSG_MORE;
2821
2822 for (buf = br_head(fconn->mbuf); b_size(buf); buf = br_del_head(fconn->mbuf)) {
2823 if (b_data(buf)) {
2824 int ret;
2825
2826 ret = conn->xprt->snd_buf(conn, conn->xprt_ctx, buf, b_data(buf), flags);
2827 if (!ret) {
2828 done = 1;
2829 break;
2830 }
2831 sent = 1;
2832 TRACE_DATA("send data", FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND, conn,,, (size_t[]){ret})trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DATA, ((1ULL << 2)), &trace_fcgi,
({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2832"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "2832") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2832" == (void *
)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x)
for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), ((void*)0), conn,
((void*)0),((void*)0),(size_t[]){ret},((void*)0), ({ char *__x
= (void *)("send data"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("send data") ? ((void *)"send data" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }));
2833 b_del(buf, ret);
2834 if (b_data(buf)) {
2835 done = 1;
2836 break;
2837 }
2838 }
2839 b_free(buf);
2840 released++;
2841 }
2842
2843 if (released)
2844 offer_buffers(NULL((void*)0), tasks_run_queue);
2845
2846 /* wrote at least one byte, the buffer is not full anymore */
2847 if (fconn->flags & (FCGI_CF_MUX_MFULL0x00000002 | FCGI_CF_DEM_MROOM0x00000010))
2848 TRACE_STATE("fconn mbuf ring not fill anymore", FCGI_EV_FCONN_SEND|FCGI_EV_FCONN_BLK, conn)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_STATE, ((1ULL << 2)|(1ULL << 3)
), &trace_fcgi, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":"
"2848"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "2848") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":"
"2848" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t
__l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }),
((void*)0), conn,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0)
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("fconn mbuf ring not fill anymore")
; (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("fconn mbuf ring not fill anymore"
) ? ((void *)"fconn mbuf ring not fill anymore" == (void *)0)
? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for
(__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
2849 fconn->flags &= ~(FCGI_CF_MUX_MFULL0x00000002 | FCGI_CF_DEM_MROOM0x00000010);
2850 }
2851
2852 if (conn->flags & CO_FL_SOCK_WR_SH) {
2853 /* output closed, nothing to send, clear the buffer to release it */
2854 b_reset(br_tail(fconn->mbuf));
2855 }
2856 /* We're not full anymore, so we can wake any task that are waiting
2857 * for us.
2858 */

3058static int fcgi_ctl(struct connection *conn, enum mux_ctl_type mux_ctl, void *output)
3059{
3060 int ret = 0;
3061 switch (mux_ctl) {
3062 case MUX_STATUS:
3063 if (!(conn->flags & CO_FL_WAIT_XPRT))
3064 ret |= MUX_STATUS_READY(1 << 0);
3065 return ret;
3066 default:
3067 return -1;
3068 }
3069}

3071/* Connection timeout management. The principle is that if there's no receipt
3072 * nor sending for a certain amount of time, the connection is closed. If the
3073 * MUX buffer still has lying data or is not allocatable, the connection is
3074 * immediately killed. If it's allocatable and empty, we attempt to send a
3075 * ABORT records.
3076 */

for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, (fconn
? fconn->conn : ((void*)0)),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*
)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x = (void *)("entering"); (struct ist
){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("entering") ? ((void
*)"entering" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t
__l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }));
3083
3084 if (!expired && fconn) {

3165
3166/* Append the description of what is present in error snapshot <es> into <out>.
3167 * The description must be small enough to always fit in a buffer. The output
3168 * buffer may be the trash so the trash must not be used inside this function.
3169 */
3170static void fcgi_show_error_snapshot(struct buffer *out, const struct error_snapshot *es)
3171{
3172 chunk_appendf(out,
3173 " FCGI connection flags 0x%08x, FCGI stream flags 0x%08x\n"
3174 " H1 msg state %s(%d), H1 msg flags 0x%08x\n"
3175 " H1 chunk len %lld bytes, H1 body len %lld bytes :\n",
3176 es->ctx.h1.c_flags, es->ctx.h1.s_flags,
3177 h1m_state_str(es->ctx.h1.state), es->ctx.h1.state,
3178 es->ctx.h1.m_flags, es->ctx.h1.m_clen, es->ctx.h1.m_blen);
3179}
3180/*
3181 * Capture a bad response and archive it in the proxy's structure. By default
3182 * it tries to report the error position as h1m->err_pos. However if this one is
3183 * not set, it will then report h1m->next, which is the last known parsing
3184 * point. The function is able to deal with wrapping buffers. It always displays
3185 * buffers as a contiguous area starting at buf->p. The direction is determined
3186 * thanks to the h1m's flags.
3187 */
3188static void fcgi_strm_capture_bad_message(struct fcgi_conn *fconn, struct fcgi_strm *fstrm,
3189 struct h1m *h1m, struct buffer *buf)
3190{
3191 struct session *sess = fstrm->sess;
3192 struct proxy *proxy = fconn->proxy;
3193 struct proxy *other_end;
3194 union error_snapshot_ctx ctx;
3195
3196 if (fstrm->cs && fstrm->cs->data) {
3197 if (sess == NULL((void*)0))
3198 sess = si_strm(fstrm->cs->data)->sess;
3199 if (!(h1m->flags & H1_MF_RESP0x00000004))
3200 other_end = si_strm(fstrm->cs->data)->be;
3201 else
3202 other_end = sess->fe;
3203 } else
3204 other_end = NULL((void*)0);
3205 /* http-specific part now */
3206 ctx.h1.state = h1m->state;
3207 ctx.h1.c_flags = fconn->flags;
3208 ctx.h1.s_flags = fstrm->flags;
3209 ctx.h1.m_flags = h1m->flags;
3210 ctx.h1.m_clen = h1m->curr_len;
3211 ctx.h1.m_blen = h1m->body_len;
3212
3213 proxy_capture_error(proxy, 1, other_end, fconn->conn->target, sess, buf, 0, 0,
3214 (h1m->err_pos >= 0) ? h1m->err_pos : h1m->next,
3215 &ctx, fcgi_show_error_snapshot);
3216}

3444/* Retrieves the first valid conn_stream from this connection, or returns NULL.
3445 * We have to scan because we may have some orphan streams. It might be
3446 * beneficial to scan backwards from the end to reduce the likeliness to find
3447 * orphans.
3448 */
3449static const struct conn_stream *fcgi_get_first_cs(const struct connection *conn)
3450{
3451 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = conn->ctx;
3452 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm;
3453 struct eb32_node *node;
3454
3455 node = eb32_first(&fconn->streams_by_id);
3456 while (node) {
3457 fstrm = container_of(node, struct fcgi_strm, by_id)((struct fcgi_strm *)(((void *)(node)) - ((long)&((struct
fcgi_strm *)0)->by_id)));
3458 if (fstrm->cs)
3459 return fstrm->cs;
3460 node = eb32_next(node);
3461 }
3462 return NULL((void*)0);
3463}

3700/* This is the tasklet referenced in fstrm->shut_tl, it is used for
3701 * deferred shutdowns when the fcgi_detach() was done but the mux buffer was full
3702 * and prevented the last record from being emitted.
3703 */
3704static struct task *fcgi_deferred_shut(struct task *t, void *ctx, unsigned short state)
3705{
3706 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm = ctx;
3707 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = fstrm->fconn;
3708
3709 TRACE_ENTER(FCGI_EV_STRM_SHUT, fconn->conn, fstrm)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 35)), &trace_fcgi
, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "3709"); (struct
ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p("src/mux_fcgi.c"
":" "3709") ? ((void *)"src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "3709" == (void *
)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x)
for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, fconn
->conn,fstrm,((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x
= (void *)("entering"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("entering") ? ((void *)"entering" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen
(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0; if (__x) for (__l--; __x[++__l]; )
; __l; }) }; }));
3710
3711 if (fstrm->flags & FCGI_SF_NOTIFIED0x00000400) {
3712 /* some data processing remains to be done first */
3713 goto end;
3714 }
3715
3716 if (fstrm->flags & FCGI_SF_WANT_SHUTW0x00002000)
3717 fcgi_do_shutw(fstrm);
3718
3719 if (fstrm->flags & FCGI_SF_WANT_SHUTR0x00001000)
3720 fcgi_do_shutr(fstrm);
3721
3722 if (!(fstrm->flags & (FCGI_SF_WANT_SHUTR0x00001000|FCGI_SF_WANT_SHUTW0x00002000))) {
3723 /* We're done trying to send, remove ourself from the send_list */
3724 LIST_DEL_INIT(&fstrm->send_list)({ typeof(&fstrm->send_list) __ret = (&fstrm->send_list
); typeof(__ret->n) __n = __ret->n; typeof(__ret->p)

for (__l--; __x[++__l]; ) ; __l; }) }; }), __FUNCTION__, ((void
*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0),((void*)0), ({ char *__x
= (void *)("leaving"); (struct ist){ .ptr = __x, .len = __builtin_constant_p
("leaving") ? ((void *)"leaving" == (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen

3764/* Called from the upper layer, to subscribe <es> to events <event_type>. The
3765 * event subscriber <es> is not allowed to change from a previous call as long
3766 * as at least one event is still subscribed. The <event_type> must only be a
3767 * combination of SUB_RETRY_RECV and SUB_RETRY_SEND. It always returns 0.
3768 */
3769static int fcgi_subscribe(struct conn_stream *cs, int event_type, struct wait_event *es)
3770{
3771 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm = cs->ctx;
3772 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = fstrm->fconn;
3773
3774 BUG_ON(event_type & ~(SUB_RETRY_SEND|SUB_RETRY_RECV));
3775 BUG_ON(fstrm->subs && fstrm->subs != es);
3776
3777 es->events |= event_type;
3778 fstrm->subs = es;
3779
3780 if (event_type & SUB_RETRY_RECV)
3781 TRACE_DEVEL("unsubscribe(recv)", FCGI_EV_STRM_RECV, fconn->conn, fstrm)trace(TRACE_LEVEL_DEVELOPER, ((1ULL << 31)), &trace_fcgi

3791/* Called from the upper layer, to unsubscribe <es> from events <event_type>
3792 * (undo fcgi_subscribe). The <es> pointer is not allowed to differ from the one
3793 * passed to the subscribe() call. It always returns zero.
3794 */
3795static int fcgi_unsubscribe(struct conn_stream *cs, int event_type, struct wait_event *es)
3796{

3802

, ({ char *__x = (void *)("src/mux_fcgi.c" ":" "3808"); (struct

== (void *)0) ? 0 : __builtin_strlen(__x) : ({ size_t __l = 0

3991

3997 }
3998

4000 htx_to_buf(htx, buf);

4017/* for debugging with CLI's "show fd" command */
4018static void fcgi_show_fd(struct buffer *msg, struct connection *conn)
4019{
4020 struct fcgi_conn *fconn = conn->ctx;
4021 struct fcgi_strm *fstrm = NULL((void*)0);
4022 struct eb32_node *node;
4023 int send_cnt = 0;
4024 int tree_cnt = 0;
4025 int orph_cnt = 0;
4026 struct buffer *hmbuf, *tmbuf;
4027
4028 if (!fconn)
4029 return;
4030
4031 list_for_each_entry(fstrm, &fconn->send_list, send_list)for (fstrm = ((typeof(fstrm))(((const char *)((&fconn->
send_list)->n)) - ((size_t)&((typeof(fstrm))((void*)0)
)->send_list))); &fstrm->send_list != (&fconn->
send_list); fstrm = ((typeof(fstrm))(((const char *)(fstrm->
send_list.n)) - ((size_t)&((typeof(fstrm))((void*)0))->
send_list))))
4032 send_cnt++;
4033
4034 fstrm = NULL((void*)0);
4035 node = eb32_first(&fconn->streams_by_id);
4036 while (node) {
4037 fstrm = container_of(node, struct fcgi_strm, by_id)((struct fcgi_strm *)(((void *)(node)) - ((long)&((struct
fcgi_strm *)0)->by_id)));
4038 tree_cnt++;
4039 if (!fstrm->cs)
4040 orph_cnt++;
4041 node = eb32_next(node);
4042 }
4043
4044 hmbuf = br_head(fconn->mbuf);
4045 tmbuf = br_tail(fconn->mbuf);
4046 chunk_appendf(msg, " fconn.st0=%d .maxid=%d .flg=0x%04x .nbst=%u"
4047 " .nbcs=%u .send_cnt=%d .tree_cnt=%d .orph_cnt=%d .sub=%d "
4048 ".dsi=%d .dbuf=%u@%p+%u/%u .mbuf=[%u..%u|%u],h=[%u@%p+%u/%u],t=[%u@%p+%u/%u]",
4049 fconn->state, fconn->max_id, fconn->flags,
4050 fconn->nb_streams, fconn->nb_cs, send_cnt, tree_cnt, orph_cnt,
4051 fconn->wait_event.events, fconn->dsi,
4052 (unsigned int)b_data(&fconn->dbuf), b_orig(&fconn->dbuf),
4053 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(&fconn->dbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(&fconn->dbuf),
4054 br_head_idx(fconn->mbuf), br_tail_idx(fconn->mbuf), br_size(fconn->mbuf),
4055 (unsigned int)b_data(hmbuf), b_orig(hmbuf),
4056 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(hmbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(hmbuf),
4057 (unsigned int)b_data(tmbuf), b_orig(tmbuf),
4058 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(tmbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(tmbuf));
4059
4060 if (fstrm) {
4061 chunk_appendf(msg, " last_fstrm=%p .id=%d .flg=0x%04x .rxbuf=%u@%p+%u/%u .cs=%p",
4062 fstrm, fstrm->id, fstrm->flags,
4063 (unsigned int)b_data(&fstrm->rxbuf), b_orig(&fstrm->rxbuf),
4064 (unsigned int)b_head_ofs(&fstrm->rxbuf), (unsigned int)b_size(&fstrm->rxbuf),
4065 fstrm->cs);
4066 if (fstrm->cs)
4067 chunk_appendf(msg, " .cs.flg=0x%08x .cs.data=%p",
4068 fstrm->cs->flags, fstrm->cs->data);
4069 }
4070}
4071
4072/* Migrate the the connection to the current thread.
4073 * Return 0 if successful, non-zero otherwise.
4074 * Expected to be called with the old thread lock held.
4075 */
4076static int fcgi_takeover(struct connection *conn)
4077{
4078 struct fcgi_conn *fcgi = conn->ctx;
4079
4080 if (fd_takeover(conn->handle.fd, conn) != 0)
4081 return -1;
4082 if (fcgi->wait_event.events)
4083 fcgi->conn->xprt->unsubscribe(fcgi->conn, fcgi->conn->xprt_ctx,
4084 fcgi->wait_event.events, &fcgi->wait_event);
4085 /* To let the tasklet know it should free itself, and do nothing else,
4086 * set its context to NULL;
4087 */
4088 fcgi->wait_event.tasklet->context = NULL((void*)0);
4089 tasklet_wakeup(fcgi->wait_event.tasklet);
4090 if (fcgi->task) {
4091 fcgi->task->context = NULL((void*)0);
4092 /* Wake the task, to let it free itself */
4093 task_wakeup(fcgi->task, TASK_WOKEN_OTHER0x4000);
4094
4095 fcgi->task = task_new(tid_bit);
4096 if (!fcgi->task) {
4097 fcgi_release(fcgi);
4098 return -1;
4099 }
4100 fcgi->task->process = fcgi_timeout_task;
4101 fcgi->task->context = fcgi;
4102 }
4103 fcgi->wait_event.tasklet = tasklet_new();
4104 if (!fcgi->wait_event.tasklet) {
4105 fcgi_release(fcgi);
4106 return -1;
4107 }
4108 fcgi->wait_event.tasklet->process = fcgi_io_cb;
4109 fcgi->wait_event.tasklet->context = fcgi;
4110 fcgi->conn->xprt->subscribe(fcgi->conn, fcgi->conn->xprt_ctx,
4111 SUB_RETRY_RECV, &fcgi->wait_event);
4112
4113 return 0;
4114}
